R, r¹
/ɑ:(r) ||; ɑr/noun [C,U] (plural R's;r's /ɑ:z ||; ɑrz/) the eighteenth letter of the English alphabet 英语字母表的第十八个字母: ‘Rabbit’ begins with an ‘R’. rabbit以字母R开头。

abbr river 河；河流: R Thames 泰晤士河

*rabbit
/ˈræbɪt ||; ˈræbɪt/noun [C] a small animal with long ears 兔: a wild rabbit 野兔 a rabbit hutch (= a cage for rabbits) 兔笼 ☞The children's word for a rabbit is bunny. 儿语称兔为bunny。

noun [C] a system of holes and underground tunnels where wild rabbits live 野兔窝

RAC
/ˌɑ:r eɪ ˈsi: ||; ˌɑr e ˈsi/abbr (Brit 英) the Royal Automobile Club; an organization for motorists. If you are a member of the RAC and your car breaks down, you can phone them and they will send sb to help you. 皇家汽车俱乐部（成员的汽车在路上发生故障，可打电话请该组织协助）

*race¹
/reɪs ||; res/noun
1 [C] a race (against/with sb/sth);a race for sth/to do sth a competition between people, animals, cars etc to see which is the fastest or to see which can achieve sth first 速度比赛；赛跑；赛马；赛车: to run/win/lose a race 参加╱赢得╱输掉一场赛跑 to come first/second/last in a race 在赛跑中跑第一╱第二╱最后 the race for the presidency 总统竞选 the race to find a cure for Aids 尽快找出艾滋病的治疗方法 Rescuing victims of the earthquake is now a race against time. 抢救地震灾民现在刻不容缓。
2 the races [pl] (Brit 英) an occasion when a number of horse races are held in one place 赛马
In Britain going to horse races and dog races is very popular. People often bet with a bookie on the result of a race. 在英国，看赛马及赛狗是很流行的。人们经常与赌注登记经纪人(bookie)赌(bet)比赛的结果。
3 [C,U] one of the groups into which people can be divided according to the colour of their skin, their hair type, the shape of their face, etc 人种；种族 ☞Look at human race. 参看human race。
4 [C] a group of people who have the same language, customs, history, etc 民族
the rat race→RAT
*race²
/reɪs ||; res/verb
1 [I,T] race (against/with sb/sth);race sb/sth to have a competition with sb/sth to find out who is the fastest or to see who can do sth first 与…比赛速度；赛跑 · I'll race you home. 我跟你比赛，看谁先跑回家。 In the 5000 metres he'll be racing against some of the finest runners in the country.
2 [I,T] to go very fast or to move sb/sth very fast 跑；疾走；使很快地移动: We raced up the stairs. 我们奔上楼梯。 The child had to be raced to hospital. 那小孩得火速送往医院。
3 [T] to make an animal or a vehicle take part in a race 使（动物或汽车）进行速度比赛

rack¹
/ræk ||; ræk/noun [C] (often in compounds 常用于构成复合词) a piece of equipment, usually made of bars, that you can put things in or on （放置对象的）架子: I got on the train and put my bags up in the luggage rack. 我登上火车，把包放在行李架上。 We need a roof rack on the car for all this luggage. 我们需要一个车顶架来放所有这些行李。 ☞picture at laboratory 见laboratory插图 go to rack and ruin to be in or get into a bad state because of a lack of care （因缺乏照料而）变坏，一团糟；年久失修而毁坏

2 [C] an illegal way of making money 非法的赚钱方法；非法勾当: a drugs racket 贩毒的勾当
3 (also racquet) [C] a piece of sports equipment that you use to hit the ball with in sports such as tennis and BADMINTON （网球、羽毛球等的）球拍 ☞Rackets are different from bats because they have strings. racket与球棒或球板(bat)不同，上有网线(string)。 ☞picture at sport 见sport插图

radar
/ˈreɪdɑ:(r) ||; ˈredɑr/noun [U] a system that uses radio waves for finding the position of moving objects, for example ships and planes 雷达: This plane is hard to detect by radar. 这种飞机雷达很难发现。 ☞Compare sonar. 与sonar比较。

radiant
/ˈreɪdiənt ||; ˈredɪənt/adj
1 showing great happiness 洋溢着幸福的；喜气洋洋的: a radiant smile 幸福的微笑
2 sending out light or heat 发光的；发热的；辐射的: the radiant heat/energy of the sun 太阳的辐射热╱辐射能

radiate
/ˈreɪdieɪt ||; ˈredɪˌet/verb
1 [T] (used about people) to clearly show a particular quality or emotion in your appearance or behaviour （指人）流露，显示（某种特性或情绪）: She radiated self-confidence in the interview. 她在面试中显示出自信。
2 [T] to send out light or heat 发出（光或热）
3 [I] to go out in all directions from a central point 由中心向四面八方伸展；呈辐射状: Narrow streets radiate from the village square. 狭窄的街道从村里的广场向四面八方伸展开去。

radiation
/ˌreɪdiˈeɪʃn ||; ˌredɪˈeʃən/noun[U]
1 powerful and very dangerous rays that are sent out from certain substances. You cannot see or feel radiation but it can cause serious illness or death 辐射 ☞Look at radioactive. 参看radioactive。
2 heat, light or energy that is sent out from sth 放热；发光；辐射能: ultraviolet radiation 紫外线辐射

radiator
/ˈreɪdieɪtə(r) ||; ˈredɪˌetɚ/noun[C]
1 a piece of equipment that is usually fixed to the wall and is used for heating a room. Radiators are made of metal and filled with hot water. 暖气装置 ☞picture on page C7 见C7页插图
2 a piece of equipment that is used for keeping a car engine cool 引擎散热器

radical¹
/ˈrædɪkl ||; ˈrædɪkḷ/adj
1 (used about changes in sth) very great; complete （指变化）很大的，彻底的: The tax system needs radical reform. 税制须要彻底改革。 radical change 彻底的改变
2 wanting great social or political change 激进的；偏激的: to have radical views 持激进观点 ☞Look at moderate ¹(2) and extreme (2). 参看moderate^1(2)及extreme(2)。 ➔radically /-kli ||; -klɪ/ adv The First World War radically altered the political map of Europe. 第一次世界大战彻底改变了欧洲的政治地图。

*radio
/ˈreɪdiəʊ ||; ˈredɪˌo/noun (plural radios)
1 oftenthe radio [U] [sing] the activity of sending out programmes for people to listen to; the programmes that are sent out 无线电广播；电台节目: I always listen to the radio in the car. 我经常在车内收听无线电广播。 I heard an interesting report on the radio this morning. 今早我从广播中收听到一则有趣的报道。 a radio station/programme 电台；电台节目 national/local radio 全国性╱地区性广播
2 [C] a piece of equipment that is used for receiving and/or sending radio messages or programmes (on a ship, plane, etc or in your house) 收音机；无线电设备 You may put, switch or turn a radio on or off. You may also turn it up or down to make it louder or quieter. 开收音机叫做put／switch／turn a radio on；关收音机叫做put／switch／turn a radio off。调高音量叫做turn it up；调低音量叫做turn it down。
3 [U] the sending or receiving of messages through the air by electrical signals 无线电传送: to keep in radio contact 以无线电保持联络 radio signals/waves 无线电信号；无线电波 radio verb [I,T] (past tense past participle radioed)

radio-
/ˈreɪdiəʊ ||; ˈredɪˌo/prefix (used in nouns, adjectives and adverbs 用于构成名词、形容词及副词)
1 connected with radio waves or the activity of sending out radio or television programmes (broadcasting) 与无线电波或无线电广播有关的: a radio-controlled car 无线电操纵的汽车
2 connected with RADIOACTIVITY(= powerful and very dangerous rays that are produced when atoms are broken up) 与放射性有关的: radiographer X射线摄影师

radioactive
/ˌreɪdiəʊˈæktɪv ||; ˌredɪoˈæktɪv/adj sending out powerful and very dangerous rays that are produced when atoms are broken up. These rays cannot be seen or felt but can cause serious illness or death. 放射性的: the problem of the disposal of radioactive waste from power stations 发电站放射性废料的处理问题 ☞Look at radiation. 参看radiation。 ➔radioactivity /ˌreɪdiəʊækˈtɪvəti ||; ˈredɪˌoækˈtɪvətɪ/ noun [U]

radius

rage²

2 (used about a battle, disease, storm, etc) to continue with great force （指战役、疾病、风暴等）剧烈地持续，肆虐: The battle raged for several days. 这场战役激烈地持续了几天。 ➔raging adj (only before a noun 只用于名词前) a raging headache 剧烈的头痛

*rain¹
/reɪn ||; ren/noun

*rain²
/reɪn ||; ren/verb
1 [I] (used with it 与it连用) to fall as rain 下雨；降雨: Oh no! It's raining again! 糟了，又下雨了！ Is it raining hard ? 雨下得大吗？ We'll go out when it stops raining. 雨停了我们便出去。
2 [I,T] rain (sth) (down) (on sb/sth) to fall or make sth fall on sb/sth in large quantities （使）大量落下: Bombs rained down on the city. 炸弹朝这个城市倾泻。
be rained off to be cancelled or to have to stop because it is raining 因下雨而取消或被逼停止: The tennis was rained off. 网球赛因下雨而取消了。

*raise
/reɪz ||; rez/verb[T]
1 to lift sth up 举起: If you want to leave the room raise your hand. 想离开房间的人请举手。 He raised himself up on one elbow. 他用一个肘撑起身体。
2 raise sth (to sth) to increase the level of sth or to make sth better or stronger 提高；增加；改善；改进: to raise taxes/salaries/prices 提高税收；增加工资；涨价 The hotel needs to raise its standards. 这家旅馆须要提高服务水平。 There's no need to raise your voice (= speak loudly or angrily). 你没必要提高嗓门。 [OPP] for senses 1 and 2lower 第1及2义的反义词皆为lower。
3 to get money from people for a particular purpose 筹款；募款: We are doing a sponsored walk to raise money for charity. 我们将参加慈善步行活动，为慈善事业筹款。 a fund-raisingevent 筹集资金的活动
4 to introduce a subject that needs to be talked about or dealt with 提出（须要讨论或处理的问题）: I would like to raise the subject of money. 我想提出金钱方面的问题。 This raises the question of why nothing was done before. 这引出了一个问题，就是为什么以前没有采取任何行动。
5 to cause a particular reaction or emotion 引起某种反应或情绪: The neighbours raised the alarm (= told everybody there was a fire/an emergency) when they saw smoke coming out of the window. 邻居看见浓烟从窗口冒出，就发出警报。 to raise hopes/fears/suspicionsin people's minds 令人们产生希望╱恐惧╱怀疑
6 to look after a child or an animal until he/she is an adult 抚养（孩子）；照料（动物）: You can't raise a family on what I earn. 我赚的钱不够养家。 ☞Look at bring sb up. 参看bring sb up。
7 to breed animals or grow a particular plant for a specific purpose （为特定目的）饲养（动物），栽种（植物）
raise your eyebrows to show that you are surprised or that you do not approve of sth （表示惊讶或不赞同时）抬起眉毛

*range¹
/reɪndʒ ||; rendʒ/noun
1 [C] [usu.sing] a range (of sth) a variety of things that belong to the same group （同一组中的）一系列事物: The course will cover a whole range of topics. 课程将涵盖一系列的主题。 This shop has a very wide range of clothes. 这家商店的衣服款式应有尽有。
2 [C] the limits between which sth can vary 范围；幅度: That car is outside my price range. 那汽车的价钱超出我能负担的价格范围。 I don't think this game is suitable for all age ranges. 我不认为这个游戏老少咸宜。
3 [C,U] the distance that it is possible for sb/sth to travel, see, hear, etc 可达到的距离；视力或听力范围: Keep out of range of the guns. 不要进入那些大炮的射程范围内。 The gunman shot the policeman at close range. 枪手在近距离射击那名警察。 They can pick up signals at a range of 400 metres. 他们可在400米的范围内接收到信号。
4 [C] a line of mountains or hills 山脉

2 range (from A to B) to include a variety of things in addition to those mentioned （除提及的以外）包括多种不同事物

*rate¹
/reɪt ||; ret/noun[C]
1 a measurement of the speed at which sth happens or the number of times sth happens or exists during a particular period 率；比率: The birth rate (= the number of children born each year) is falling. 出生率在下降。 The population is increasing at the rate of less than 0.5% a year. 每年的人口增长率不到0.5%。 an exchange rateof one pound to ten francs 一英镑兑十法郎的汇率
2 a fixed amount of money that sth costs or that sb is paid 费用；价格: The basic rate of pay is £10 an hour. 基本工资一小时10英镑。 We offer special reduced rates for students. 我们给予学生特别优惠价。 ☞ Look at first-rate and second-rate. 参看first-rate及second-rate。
at any rate(spoken 口语)
1 used when you are giving more exact information about sth （用于补充更确切的资料）: He said that they would be here by ten. At any rate, I think that's what he said. 他说过他们在十时到达这里。反正，我想他是这样说的。
2 whatever else might happen 无论如何；不管怎样: Well, that's one good piece of news at any rate. 好了，无论如何，那是个好消息。
the going rate (for sth)→GOING²
rate²
/reɪt ||; ret/verb (not used in the continuous tenses 不用于进行时)
1 [I,T] to say how good you think sb/sth is 评价: She's rated among the best tennis players of all time. 她被评为有史以来最佳的网球选手之一。 The match rated as one of their worst defeats. 这场比赛被认为是他们的惨败之一。
2 [T] to be good, important, etc enough to be treated in a particular way 值得；应得: The accident wasn't very serious -- it didn't rate a mention in the local newspaper. 那起事故并不太严重，本地报纸提都没提。

*rather
/ˈrɑ:ðə(r); US ˈræ- ||; ˈræðɚ/adv quite; to some extent 颇；相当程度上: It was a rather nice day. 那天的天气相当不错。 It was rather a nice day. 那天的天气相当不错。 It cost rather a lot of money. 那花去了很多的钱。 I was rather hoping that you'd be free on Friday. 我很希望你星期五有空。 ☞ Fairly, quite, rather and pretty can all mean ‘not very’. Fairly is the weakest. Rather and pretty (informal) are the strongest. Fairly and quite are mostly used with words that are positive The room was fairly tidy. Rather is used when you are criticizing sth This room's rather untidy. If you use rather with a positive word, it sounds as if you are surprised and pleased The new teacher is actually rather nice, though he doesn't look very friendly. fairly、quite、rather及pretty均表示“不太”或“适度”。fairly语气最弱。rather及pretty（非正式）的语气最强。fairly及quite大多与肯定的词连用：The room was fairly tidy.这房间颇为整洁。rather用于批评：This room's rather untidy.这房间相当凌乱。rather若与肯定的词连用，则含有令人惊喜的意思：The new teacher is actually rather nice, though he doesn't look very friendly.新老师其实人很好，虽然他样子不太友善。 or rather used as a way of correcting sth you have said, or making it more exact （用于更正或进一步说清楚刚才说的话）: She lives in London, or rather she lives in a suburb of London. 她住在伦敦，更确切地说，是伦敦近郊。 rather than instead of; in place of 取代；不是: I think I'll just have a sandwich rather than a full meal. 我想我只要一份三明治，不要全餐。 would rather... (than) would prefer to 宁愿: I'd rather go to the cinema than watch television. 与其看电视，我宁愿去看电影。

ratify
/ˈrætɪfaɪ ||; ˈrætəˌfaɪ/verb [T] (present participle ratifying third person singular present ratifies;past tense past participle ratified) to make an agreement officially acceptable by voting for or signing it 正式批准；签字认可 ➔ratification /ˌrætɪfɪˈkeɪʃn ||; ˌrætəfəˈkeʃən/ noun [U]: The agreement is subject to ratification by the Senate. 这项协议要经参议院批准。

/ˈreɪʃiəʊ ||; ˈreʃɪˌo/noun [C] ratio (of A to B) the relation between two numbers which shows how much bigger one quantity is than another 比例；比率: The ratio of boys to girls in this class is three to one (= there are three times as many boys as girls). 这班上的男女生的比例是三比一。

rational
/ˈræʃnəl ||; ˈræʃənḷ/adj

/ˌræʃəˈnɑ:l ||; ˌræʃəˈnæl/noun [C] (formal 正式)the rationale (behind/for/of sth) the principles or reasons which explain a particular decision, course of action, belief, etc （某决定、行动、信念等的）原则，理由: What is the rationale behind these new exams? 干吗要进行这种新的考试？

rattle sth off to say a list of things you have learned very quickly 迅速背诵: She rattled off the names of every player in the team. 她一口气说出了队中每个球员的名字。

*reach¹
/ri:tʃ ||; ritʃ/verb
1 [T] to arrive at a place or condition that you have been going towards 到达；抵达；达至；达到: We won't reach Dover before 12. 我们12点前到不了多佛尔。 The two sides hope to reach an agreement sometime today. 双方希望在今天之内达成协议。 Sometimes the temperature reaches 45°C. 气温有时达到45摄氏度。 The team reached the semi-final last year. 该球队去年进入半决赛。 to reach a decision/conclusion/compromise 作出决定；得出结论；达成妥协
2 [I,T] reach (out) (for sb/sth);reach (sth) (down) to stretch out your arm to try and touch or get sth 伸手（接触或取某物）: The child reached out for her mother. 小孩伸手要妈妈抱。 She reached into her bag for her purse. 她把手伸进手提包里拿钱包。
3 [I,T] to be able to touch sth 够得着（某物）: Can you get me that book off the top shelf? I can't reach. 你可以替我拿书架最上层那本书吗？我够不着。 He couldn't reach the light switch. 他够不着电灯开关。 I need a longer ladder. This one won't reach. 我要把长一点的梯子。这把够不着。
4 [T] to communicate with sb, especially by telephone; contact 通讯（尤指用电话）；联络: You can reach me at this number. 你可以拨这个号码找我。
reach²
/ri:tʃ ||; ritʃ/noun [U] the distance that you can stretch your arm 伸手可达的距离 beyond/out of (sb's) reach
1 outside the distance that you can stretch your arm 在伸手够不着的距离: Keep this medicine out of the reach of children. 将这药放在儿童拿不到的地方。
2 not able to be got or done by sb 不能得到或做到；能力范围以外: A job like that is completely beyond his reach. 像那样的一份工作他完全不能胜任。
within (sb's) reach
1 inside the distance that you can stretch your arm 在伸手可及的距离内
2 able to be achieved by sb 能够做到；能力范围以内: We were one goal ahead with ten minutes left and so could sense that victory was within our reach. 还剩下十分钟的时候，我们领先一球，所以我们觉得已经胜利在望了。
within (easy) reach of sth not far from sth 离某物不远

*react
/riˈækt ||; rɪˈækt/verb[I]
1 react (to sth) (by doing sth) to do or say sth because of sth that has happened or been said 作出反应；回应: He reacted to the news by jumping up and down and shouting. 他一听到这消息就跳上跳下，大喊大叫。 The players reacted angrily to the decision. 球员们对这个决定很生气。
2 react (to sth) to become ill after eating, breathing, etc a particular substance （吃或吸入某物后）觉得不舒服
3 react (with sth/together) (used about a chemical substance) to change after coming into contact with another substance （指化学物质）起化学作用
react against sb/sth to behave or talk in a way that shows that you do not like the influence of sb/sth (for example authority, your family, etc) 反对，反抗（当权者、家庭等）

*reaction
/riˈækʃn ||; rɪˈækʃən/noun
1 [C,U] (a) reaction (to sb/sth) something that you do or say because of sth that has happened 反应；回应: Could we have your reaction to the latest news, Prime Minister? 首相先生，能不能告诉我们你对这个最新消息有什么反应？ I shook him to try and wake him up but there was no reaction. 我摇摇他想把他弄醒，但他没有反应。
2 [C,U] (a) reaction (against sb/sth) behaviour that shows that you do not like the influence of sb/sth (for example authority, your family, etc) （对当权者、家庭等的）反抗，反对
3 [C] a reaction (to sth) a bad effect that your body experiences because of sth that you have eaten, touched or breathed （吃、触摸、吸入某物后产生的）不良反应，不舒服: She had an allergic reaction to something in the food. 她对食物里的某种东西有过敏反应。
4 [C] [usu.pl] the physical ability to act quickly when sth happens 本能的反应: If the other driver's reactions hadn't been so good, there would have been an accident. 如果另外那个司机的反应不这么快，早就发生事故了。
5 [C,U] (technical术语) a chemical change produced by two or more substances coming into contact with each other （两种或以上物质接触后所产生的）化学反应，化学作用

*read¹
/ri:d ||; rid/verb (past tense past participle read /red ||; rɛd/)
1 [I,T] to look at words or symbols and understand them 读；阅读；看懂: He never learnt to read and write. 他一直没有学会读书写字。 Have you read any good books lately? 你最近有没有看过什么好书？ Can you read music? 你能看懂乐谱吗？
2 [I,T] read (sb) (sth);read sth (to sb) to say written words to sb 朗读 · My father used to read me stories when I was a child. 我小时候父亲常给我读故事。 I hate reading out loud. 我讨厌大声朗读。
3 [T] to be able to understand sth from what you can see 看明白: A man came to read the gas meter. 有个男子来抄煤气表。 Profoundly deaf people train to read lips. 耳朵很背的人接受读唇的训练。 I've no idea what he'll say -- I can't read his mind! 我不知道他要说些什么─我看不透他的心思！
4 [T] to show words or a sign of sth 标明；显示；写着: The sign read ‘Keep Left’. 告示牌上写着“靠左行驶”。
5 [T] (formal 正式) to study a subject at university （在大学里）攻读（某学科）: She read Modern Languages at Cambridge. 她在剑桥大学攻读现代语言。
read sth into sth to think that there is a meaning in sth that may not really be there 假想有某种含意 read on to continue reading; to read the next part of sth 继续读；看下去 read sth out to read sth to other people 朗读；宣读；诵读 read sth through to read sth to check details or to look for mistakes 从头至尾看一遍（以检查内容或寻找错误）: I read my essay through a few times before handing it in. 我把我的文章看了几遍才交出去。 read up on sth to find out everything you can about a subject 研究；研读

*ready
/ˈredi ||; ˈrɛdɪ/adj
1 ready (for sb/sth);ready (to do sth) prepared and able to do sth or to be used 准备好；准备就绪: The car will be ready for you to collect on Friday. 汽车星期五可以备好，让你来取。 He isn't ready to take his driving test -- he hasn't had enough lessons. 他上课不足，还未准备好参加驾驶执照考试。 I'm meeting him at 7, so I don't have long to get ready. 我7点钟要跟他见面，因此没有多少时间准备了。 I'll go and get the dinner ready. 我会把晚饭准备好。 Have your money readybefore you get on the bus. 上公共汽车前先准备好车费。
2 ready to do sth;ready (with/for sth) prepared and happy to do sth 愿意；乐于: You know me -- I'm always ready to help. 你是了解我的─我随时都乐意帮忙。 Charlie's always ready with advice. 查利总是乐于给予意见。 The men were angry and ready for a fight. 那几个男子很生气，准备动手打架。 I know it's early, but I'm ready for bed. 我知道时间还早，但我准备睡觉了。
3 adv (used to form compound adjectives 用于构成复合形容词) that has already been made or done; not done especially for you 预先制成或做好；现成: ready-cooked food 预先烹调好的食物 There are no ready-made answers to this problem -- we'll have to find our own solution. 这个问题没有现成的答案─我们得自己寻找解决办法。

reaffirm
/ˌri:əˈfɜ:m ||; ˌriəˈfɝm/verb [T] (written 书面语) to state sth again in order to emphasize that it is still true 重申；再次确定

/riˈeɪdʒənt ||; riˈedʒənt/noun [C] (technical术语) a substance used to cause a chemical reaction, especially in order to find out if another substance is present 试剂

*real¹
/ˈri:əl;rɪəl||; ˈriəl/adj
1 actually existing, not imagined 现实的；存在的: The film is based on real life. 这部电影取材自现实生活。 This isn't a real word, I made it up. 这个词不是真有的，是我编造出来的。 We have a real chance of winning. 我们确实有获胜的机会。 Closure of the factory is a very real danger. 工厂倒闭是个很现实的危险。
2 actually true; not only what people think is true 真的；真正的；真实的: The name he gave to the police wasn't his real name. 他告诉警方的姓名并不是他的真实姓名。 She said she missed the bus, but that's not the real reason why she was late.
3 (only before a noun 只用于名词前) having all, not just some, of the qualities necessary to really be sth 具有一切所需特性的: She was my first real girlfriend. 她是我第一个真正的女朋友。
4 natural, not false or artificial 天然的；不是假的或人造的: This shirt is real silk. 这件衬衫是真丝制的。
5 (only before a noun 只用于名词前) (used to emphasize a state, feeling or quality) strong or big （用于强调状况、感受或特性）强大的，重大的: The meal I cooked was a real disaster. · Money is a real problem for us at the moment. 目前金钱对我们来说是个大问题。 He made a real effort to be polite. 他作了很大努力来表现得有礼貌。
for real genuine or serious 真正；认真: Her tears weren't for real. 她的眼泪并不是真心实意的。 Was he for real when he offered you the job? 他给你提供那份工作是当真的吗？ the real thing something genuine, not a copy 真迹；原作: This painting is just a copy. The real thing is in a gallery. 这幅画只是复制品，原作收藏在一家美术馆内。 She's had boyfriends before but this time she says it's the real thing (= real love). 她曾经有过一些男朋友，但她说这个才是真心所爱的。
real²
/ˈri:əl;rɪəl||; ˈriəl/adv (US 美) (informal 非正式) very; really 很；真正: It was real kind of you to help me.

realign
/ˌri:əˈlaɪn ||; ˌriəˈlaɪn/verb [T] (written 书面语)
1 to change the position or direction of sth in relation to sth else 调整位置﹙或方向﹚
2 to make changes to sth in order to adapt it to a new situation 对…进行调整以适应新形势: The company has been forced to realign its operations in the area. 公司被迫对这一领域的经营进行了调整。
3 realign yourself (with sb/sth) to change your opinions, policies, etc so that they are the same as those of another person, group, etc 改变观点，改变策略﹙使与别人一样﹚ ➔realignment noun [U,C]: the realignment of personal goals 个人目标的调整

realism
/ˈri:əlɪzəm;(brit also 英亦作) ˈrɪə- ||; ˈriəlˌɪzəm; ˈrɪə-/noun[U]
1 behaviour that shows that you accept the facts of a situation and are not influenced by your feelings 实事求是的态度；现实主义 ☞Look at idealism. 参看idealism。
2 (in art, literature, etc) showing things as they really are （艺术、文学等）现实主义，写实主义

realist
/ˈri:əlɪst;(brit also 英亦作) ˈrɪə- ||; ˈriəlɪst; ˈrɪə-/noun[C]
1 a person who accepts the facts of a situation, and does not try to pretend that it is different 实事求是的人；现实主义者: I'm a realist -- I don't expect the impossible. 我是个实事求是的人，不会期望发生不可能的事。
2 an artist or writer who shows things as they really are 现实主义画家或作家

realistic
/ˌri:əˈlɪstɪk;(brit also 英亦作) ˌrɪə- ||; ˌriəˈlɪstɪk; ˌrɪə-/adj
1 sensible and understanding what it is possible to achieve in a particular situation 实事求是的；现实的: We have to be realistic about our chances of winning. 对于我们获胜的可能性，我们要实事求是。
2 showing things as they really are 写实的: a realistic drawing/description 写生画；真实写照
3 not real but appearing to be real 逼真的；栩栩如生的: The monsters in the film were very realistic. 电影中的怪物很逼真。 ➔realistically /-kli ||; -klɪ/ adv

*reality
/riˈæləti ||; rɪˈælətɪ/noun (plural realities)
1 [U] the way life really is, not the way it may appear to be or how you would like it to be 现实: I enjoyed my holiday, but now it's back to reality. 我假期过得很愉快，但现在要返回现实了。 We have to face reality and accept that we've failed. 我们得面对现实，承认已经失败。
2 [C] a thing that is actually experienced, not just imagined 事实；实际情况: Films portray war as heroic and exciting, but the reality is very different. 电影把战争刻画得又壮烈又刺激，但事实却相差很远。
in reality in fact, really (not the way sth appears or has been described) 事实上；实际上: People say this is an exciting city but in reality it's rather boring. 人们说这是个充满刺激的城市，事实上却相当沉闷。

*realize
/ˈrɪəlaɪz ||; ˈrɪəˌlaɪz/ (also -ise) verb [T]
1 to know and understand that sth is true or that sth has happened 知道；明白；了解到: I'm sorry I mentioned it, I didn't realize how much it upset you. 我很抱歉提及那件事，我不知道会使你这样不高兴的。 Didn't you realize (that) you needed to bring money? 难道你不知道须要带钱来吗？
2 to become conscious of sth or that sth has happened, usually some time later 察觉；发觉；意识到: When I got home, I realized that I had left my keys at the office. 我回到家里才发觉把钥匙忘在办公室里了。
3 to make sth that you imagined become reality 实现；使成为现实: His worst fears were realized when he saw the damage caused by the fire. 当他看到这场大火造成的破坏，他最担心的事终于发生了。 ➔realization(also -isation) /ˌrɪəlaɪˈzeɪʃn ||; ˌrɪələˈzeʃən/ noun [U]

*really
/ˈrɪəli ||; ˈrɪəlɪ/adv
1 actually; in fact 确实；事实上；真正: I couldn't believe it was really happening. 我无法相信这事真的发生了。 He said he was sorry but I don't think he really meant it. 他说他很抱歉，但我不认为他是当真的。 She wasn't really angry, she was only pretending. 她不是真的生气，只是假装而已。 Is it really true? 真有其事吗？
2 very; very much 很；十分: I'm really tired. 我很累。 Are you really sure? 你十分有把握吗？ I really hope you enjoy yourself. 我很希望你过得愉快。 I really tried but I couldn't do it. 我努力尝试过了，但是做不来。
3 used as a question for expressing surprise, interest, doubt, etc （用作问句，表示惊奇、感兴趣、怀疑等）: ‘She's left her husband.’ ‘Really? When did that happen?’ “她已离开丈夫。”“真的吗？是在什么时候发生的？”
4 used in negative sentences to make what you are saying less strong （用于否定句中缓和说话语气）: I don't really agree with that. 我对那个不大赞成。
5 used in questions when you are expecting sb to answer ‘No’ （用于疑问句中，预料对方会作出否定的回答）: You don't really expect me to believe that, do you? 你不是真的以为我会相信那个吧？

*reason¹
/ˈri:zn ||; ˈrizṇ/noun
1 [C] a reason (for sth/for doing sth);a reason why.../that... a cause or an explanation for sth that has happened or for sth that sb has done 原因；理由: What's your reason for being so late? 你迟到了这么久有什么原因？ Is there any reason why you couldn't tell me this before? 你以前不能告诉我这件事，是不是有什么原因？ He said he couldn't come but he didn't give a reason. 他说他不能来，但没有说明原因。 The reason (that) I'm phoning you is to ask a favour. 我打电话给你是想请你帮忙。 For some reason they can't give us an answer until next week. 由于某种原因，他们要到下星期才能给我们答复。 She left the job for personal reasons. 她因私人理由离职了。
2 [C,U] (a) reason (to do sth);(a) reason (for sth/for doing sth) something that shows that it is right or fair to do sth 正当或合理的理由: I have reason to believe that you've been lying. 我有理由相信你一直在说谎。 I think we have reason for complaint. 我认为我们有理由投诉。 You have every reason (= you are completely right) to be angry, considering how badly you've been treated. 你受到那样恶劣的对待，完全有理由生气。
3 [U] the ability to think and to make sensible decisions 推理能力；理智；理性: Only human beings are capable of reason. 只有人类才有理性。
4 [U] what is right or acceptable 对的或可接受的东西；道理: I tried to persuade him not to drive but he just wouldn't listen to reason. 我试过劝他不要驾车，但他就是不听道理。 I'll pay anything within reason for a ticket. 只要价钱合理，我就会购票。
it stands to reason(informal 非正式) it is obvious if you think about it 自不待言；理所当然

/ˈri:zn ||; ˈrizṇ/verb [I,T] to form a judgement or an opinion, after thinking about sth in a logical way 推断；推论；推理 reason with sb to talk to sb in order to persuade him/her to behave or think in a more reasonable way 与某人讲道理；劝某人诉诸理性

*reasonable
/ˈri:znəbl ||; ˈriznəbḷ/adj
1 fair, practical and sensible 公平的；实际的；合情合理的: I think it's reasonable to expect people to keep their promises. 我认为期望人们遵守诺言是合乎情理的。 I tried to be reasonable even though I was very angry. 虽然我很生气，但我仍尽量讲道理。
2 acceptable and appropriate in a particular situation 可以接受的；合适的: He made us a reasonable offer for the car. 他向我们提出了合理的价钱买那辆汽车。 [OPP] unreasonable 反义词为unreasonable
3 (used about prices 指价格) not too expensive 不太贵的；公道的: We sell good quality food at reasonable prices. 我们以公道的价钱出售优质食品。
4 quite good, high, big, etc but not very 尚好的；过得去的: His work is of a reasonable standard. 他的工作水平还过得去。

*receive
/rɪˈsi:v ||; rɪˈsiv/verb[T]
1 receive sth (from sb/sth) to get or accept sth that sb sends or gives to you 收到；接到: I received a letter from an old friend last week. 我上星期收到一位老朋友的信。 to receive a phone call/a prize 接到电话；领奖
2 to experience a particular kind of treatment or injury 受到，经历（某种待遇或伤害）: We received a warm welcome from our hosts. 我们受到主人的热烈欢迎。 He received several cuts and bruises in the accident. 他在事故中受了几处割伤瘀伤。
3 (often passive 常用于被动语态) to react to sth new in a particular way （对新事物）作出某种反应: The film has been well received by the critics. 这部电影得到影评人的好评。

reˌceived pronunciˈation
=RP

receiver
/rɪˈsi:və(r) ||; rɪˈsivɚ/noun[C]
1 (also handset) the part of a telephone that is used for listening and speaking 电话听筒 To answer or make a telephone call you pick up or lift the receiver. To end a telephone call you put down or replace the receiver or you hang up. 接或打电话时要拿起(pick up／lift)听筒。谈话完毕后要放下(put down／replace)听筒或挂断(hang up)。
2 a piece of television or radio equipment that changes electronic signals into sounds or pictures 接收机；电视机；收音机

*recent
/ˈri:snt ||; ˈrisṇt/adj that happened or began only a short time ago 最近的；近来的: In recent years there have been many changes. 近几年来有很多变化。 This is a recent photograph of my daughter. 这是我女儿的近照。

*recently
/ˈri:sntli ||; ˈrisṇtlɪ/adv not long ago 不久前；近来: She worked here until quite recently. 不久之前她还在这里工作。 Have you seen Paul recently? 你最近见过保罗没有？ Recently can refer to both a point in time and a period of time. If it refers to a point in time, use the past simple tense He got married recently. If it refers to a period, use the present perfect or present perfect continuous tense I haven't done anything interesting recently. She's been working hard recently. Lately can only refer to a period of time. It is used only with the present perfect or present perfect continuous tense I've seen a lot of films lately. I've been spending too much money lately. recently可以指一个时间点或一段时间。指一个时间点，用简单过去时：He got married recently.他最近结婚了。指一段时间，则用现在完成时或现在完成进行时：I haven't done anything interesting recently.我最近没有做过什么有趣的事情。·She's been working hard recently.她近来一直很努力工作。lately只用于指一段时间，要用现在完成时或现在完成进行时：I've seen a lot of films lately.我近来看了很多部电影。·I've been spending too much money lately.我最近钱花得太多了。

2 (technical术语) the rounded area at the top of a STEM that supports the head of a flower 花托 ☞picture at flower 见flower插图

*reception
/rɪˈsepʃn ||; rɪˈsɛpʃən/noun
1 [U] the place inside the entrance of a hotel or office building where guests or visitors go when they first arrive （旅馆、办公大楼的）接待处，服务台: Leave your key at / in receptionif you go out, please. 你外出的话，请把钥匙留在接待处。 the reception desk （旅馆的）服务台
2 [C] a formal party to celebrate sth or to welcome an important person 庆祝会；欢迎会；招待会: Their wedding reception was held at a local hotel. 他们的婚礼庆祝会在本地一家旅馆举行。 There will be an official reception at the embassy for the visiting ambassador. 大使馆将有一个正式招待会，欢迎到访的大使。
3 [sing] the way people react to sth 反应: The play got a mixed reception (= some people liked it, some people didn't). 这出戏获得的评论毁誉参半。
4 [U] the quality of radio or television signals （收音机或电视的）接收效果: TV reception is very poor where we live. 在我们住的地方，电视的接收效果很差。

*recipe
/ˈresəpi ||; ˈrɛsəpɪ/noun[C]

reciprocate
/rɪˈsɪprəkeɪt ||; rɪˈsɪprəˌket/verb
1 [T] [I] (formal 正式)reciprocate (sth) (with sth) to behave or feel towards sb in the same way as he/she behaves or feels towards you 以与对方同样的方式表现或感觉；回报: Her passion for him was not reciprocated. 她对他的爱没有得到回报。 They wanted to reciprocate the kindness that had been shown to them. 他们想要报答受到过的盛情。 He smiled but his smile was not reciprocated. 他笑了，但对方没有朝他笑。
2 [I] (technical术语) to move backwards and forwards in a straight line 往复运动: a reciprocating action/movement 往复动作／运动 ➔reciprocation /rɪˌsɪprəˈkeɪʃn ||; rɪˌsɪprəˈkeʃən/ noun [U]

/ˈrekləs ||; ˈrɛklɪs/adj not thinking about possible bad or dangerous results that could come from your actions 鲁莽的；不顾后果的: reckless driving 鲁莽驾驶 ➔recklessly adv

reckon
/ˈrekən ||; ˈrɛkən/verb [T] (informal 非正式)
1 to think; to have an opinion about sth 想；认为: She's very late now. I reckon (that) she isn't coming. 她已经晚了很久。我想她不会来了。 I think she's forgotten. What do you reckon? 我想她忘了。你认为呢？
2 to calculate sth approximately 估计: I reckon the journey will take about half an hour. 我估计这趟行程将会花半小时左右。
3 to expect to do sth 预料: I wasn't reckoning to pay so much. 我没有预料到要付这么多钱。
reckon on sth to expect sth to happen and therefore to base a plan or action on it 预期某事会发生而据以作出计划或行动: I didn't book in advance because I wasn't reckoning on tickets being so scarce. 我没有预订，因为我没料到票会这么少。 reckon (sth) up to calculate the total amount or number of sth 计算（全部的数量或数目） reckon with sb/sth to think about sb/sth as a possible problem 考虑到

reckoning
/ˈrekənɪŋ ||; ˈrɛkənɪŋ/noun
1 [U] [C] the act of calculating sth, especially in a way that is not very exact 估算；估计
2 [C] [usu.sing] [U] (formal 正式) a time when sb's actions will be judged to be right or wrong and they may be punished 报应；报偿: In the final reckoning truth is rewarded. 真理最终会得到报偿。 Officials concerned with environmental policy predict that a day of reckoning will come. 环境政策官员预言，遭报应的一天总会来到。
in/into/out of the reckoning (especially Brit 尤为英) (especially in sport) among/not among those who are likely to win or be successful （尤用于体育）有╱无望取胜或成功: Greene is fit again and should come into the reckoning. 格林又状态良好，应该有望获胜。

*recognize
/ˈrekəgnaɪz ||; ˈrɛkəgˌnaɪz/ (also -ise) verb [T]
1 to know again sb/sth that you have seen or heard before 认得；辨认出: I recognized him but I couldn't remember his name. 我认得他，但记不起他的名字。
2 to accept that sth is true 承认（某事属实）
3 to accept sth officially 正式承认；认可: My qualifications are not recognized in other countries. 我的资格在其他国家不被认可。
4 to show officially that you think sth that sb has done is good 表扬

recollection
/ˌrekəˈlekʃn ||; ˌrɛkəˈlɛkʃən/noun

*recommend
/ˌrekəˈmend ||; ˌrɛkəˈmɛnd/verb[T]
1 recommend sb/sth (to sb) (for/as sth) to say that sb/sth is good and that sb should try or use him/her/it 推荐；介绍: Which film would you recommend? 你推荐哪一部电影？ Could you recommend me a good hotel? 你可以给我介绍一家好的旅馆吗？ We hope that you'll recommend this restaurant to all your friends. 我们希望你向所有朋友推荐这家餐馆。 Doctors don't always recommend drugs as the best treatment for every illness. 医生不总是认为使用药物是治疗任何疾病的最好方法。
2 to tell sb what you strongly believe he/she should do 建议；劝告: I recommend that you get some legal advice. 我建议你去咨询一下法律意见。 I wouldn't recommend (your) travelling on your own. It could be dangerous. 我劝你不要单独旅游，可能会有危险的。 ☞Look at suggest. 参看suggest。

recommendation
/ˌrekəmenˈdeɪʃn ||; ˌrɛkəmɛnˈdeʃən/noun
1 [C,U] saying that sth is good and should be tried or used 推荐；介绍: I visited Seville on a friend's recommendationand I really enjoyed it. 在朋友的推荐下，我游览了塞维利亚。我真的很喜欢那里。
2 [C] a statement about what should be done in a particular situation 建议: In their report on the crash, the committee make several recommendationson how safety could be improved. 在失事报告里，委员会提出了几项改善安全的建议。

recompense
/ˈrekəmpens ||; ˈrɛkəmˌpɛns/verb [T] (formal 正式)recompense sb (for sth) to give money, etc to sb for special efforts or work or because you are responsible for a loss he/she has suffered （以金钱等）酬劳，赔偿，补偿: The airline has agreed to recompense us for the damage to our luggage. 航空公司答应赔偿我们行李受到的损失。 recompense noun [sing] [U]: Please accept this cheque in recompense for our poor service. 请接受这张支票，作为我们服务欠佳的补偿。

reconcile
/ˈrekənsaɪl ||; ˈrɛkənˌsaɪl/verb[T]
1 reconcile sth (with sth) to find a way of dealing with two ideas, situations, statements, etc that seem to be opposite to each other 协调；调和: She finds it difficult to reconcile her career ambitions with her responsibilities to her children. 她发觉很难兼顾事业上的抱负和对子女的责任。
2 (often passive 常用于被动语态) reconcile sb (with sb) to make people become friends again after an argument 使重修旧好；使和解: After years of not speaking to each other, she and her parents were eventually reconciled. 她与父母多年来互不理睬，后来终于和好了。
3 reconcile yourself to sth to accept an unpleasant situation because there is nothing you can do to change it 无可奈何地接受 ➔reconciliation /ˌrekənsɪliˈeɪʃn ||; ˌrɛkənˌsɪlɪˈeʃən/ noun [sing] [U]: The negotiators are hoping to bring about a reconciliation between the two sides. 谈判者希望双方达成和解。

/rɪˈkɒnɪsns ||; rɪˈkɑnəsəns/noun [C,U] the study of a place or area for military reasons 侦察: The plane was shot down while on a reconnaissance mission over enemy territory. 那架飞机在敌人领土上空执行侦察任务时被击落。

reconstitute
/ˌri:ˈkɒnstɪtju:t ||; riˈkɑnstəˌtut/verb[T]
1 reconstitute sth/itself (as sth) (formal 正式) to form an organization or a group again in a different way 重组；重新设立: The group reconstituted itself as a political party. 这个团体重新组建成为一个政党。
2 (usually passive 通常用于被动语态) to bring dried food, etc back to its original form by adding water 使﹙脱水食物等﹚恢复原状；使还原: reconstituted orange juice 加水还原的橙汁

reconstruct
/ˌri:kənˈstrʌkt ||; ˌrikənˈstrʌkt/verb[T]
1 to build again sth that has been destroyed or damaged 重建（已毁坏的东西）
2 to get a full description or picture of sth using the facts that are known （用已知的事实）推想出整体情况；重视: The police are trying to reconstruct the victim's movements on the day of the murder. 警方正设法重新构想受害人在凶杀案当日的行踪。 ➔reconstruction /-ˈstrʌkʃn ||; -ˈstrʌkʃən/ noun [C,U] a reconstruction of the crime using actors 由演员重演作案过程

*record¹
/ˈrekɔ:d; US ˈrekərd ||; ˈrɛkɚd/noun
1 [C] a record (of sth) a written account of what has happened, been done, etc 记录；记载: The teachers keep records of the children's progress. 老师把孩子们的进步情况记录下来。 medical records 病历
2 [sing] the facts, events, etc that are known (and sometimes written down) about sb/sth 档案数据；履历；记录: The police said that the man had a criminal record (= he had been found guilty of crimes in the past). 警方说那人有犯罪记录。 This airline has a bad safety record. 这家航空公司的安全记录不佳。
3 [C] (also album) a thin, round piece of plastic which can store music so that you can play it when you want 唱片
4 [C] the best performance or the highest or lowest level, etc ever reached in sth, especially in sport 纪录，最高成绩，最高或最低水平（尤指体育方面的）: Who holds the world record forhigh jump? 谁是跳高的世界纪录保持者？ She's hoping to break the record for the 100 metres. 她希望打破100米赛跑的纪录。 He did it in record time (= very fast). 他以破纪录的时间完成。
be/go on (the) record (as saying...) to say sth publicly or officially so that it may be written down and repeated 公开或正式说: He didn't want to go on the record as either praising or criticizing the proposal. 他不想公开赞扬或批评这个建议。 off the record if you tell sb sth off the record, it is not yet official and you do not want it to be repeated publicly 非正式；非公开: She told me off the record that she was going to resign. 她私下对我说，她要辞职。 put/set the record straight to correct a mistake by telling sb the true facts （说出正确事实以）纠正错误
*record²
/rɪˈkɔ:d ||; rɪˈkɔrd/verb
1 [T] to write down or film facts or events so that they can be referred to later and will not be forgotten 记下；记录；记载: He recorded everything in his diary. 他在日记里把什么都记下了。 At the inquest the coroner recorded a verdict of accidental death. 验尸时，法医判定是意外死亡，并记录在案。
2 [I,T] to put music, a film, a programme, etc onto a CD or cassette so that it can be listened to or watched again later 录音；录像: Quiet, please! We're recording. 请肃静！我们正在录音。 The band has recently recorded a new album. 该乐队最近录制了一张新唱片。 There's a concert I would like to record from the radio this evening. 今晚电台播放一场音乐会，我想把它录下来。

ˈrecord-breaking
adj (only before a noun 只用于名词前) the best, fastest, highest, etc ever 破纪录的；空前的: We did the journey in record-breaking time. 我们在破纪录的时间内完成了旅程。

/rɪˈkɔ:də(r) ||; rɪˈkɔrdɚ/noun[C]

2 a type of musical instrument that is often played by children. You play it by blowing through it and covering the holes in it with your fingers. 竖笛 ☞Look at the note at piano. 参看piano的注释。 ☞picture at music 见music插图

recording
/rɪˈkɔ:dɪŋ ||; rɪˈkɔrdɪŋ/noun
1 [C] sound or pictures that have been put onto a cassette, CD, film, etc 录音；录像: the Berlin Philharmonic's recording of Mahler's Sixth symphony 柏林爱乐交响乐团演奏马勒第六交响曲的录音
2 [U] the process of making a cassette, record, film, etc 录制（盒式录音带、唱片、影片等）: a recording session/studio 一场录音；录音室；录像棚

ˈrecord player
noun [C] a machine that you use for playing records （电）唱机；留声机

recount
/rɪˈkaʊnt ||; rɪˈkaυnt/verb [T] (formal 正式) to tell a story or describe an event 叙述；讲述

recoup
/rɪˈku:p ||; rɪˈkup/verb [T] to get back an amount of money that you have spent or lost 收回﹙成本﹚；弥补﹙亏损﹚: We hope to recoup our initial investment in the first year. 我们希望我们的前期投资在第一年就能赚回来。

recourse
/rɪˈkɔ:s ||; rɪˈkɔrs/noun [C] (formal 正式) having to use sth or ask sb for help in a difficult situation （在困难情况下）需要某人或某物的帮助: She made a complete recovery without recourse to surgery. 她没有动手术就完全康复了。

*recover
/rɪˈkʌvə(r) ||; rɪˈkʌvɚ/verb
1 [I] recover (from sth) to become well again after you have been ill 康复；复原；痊愈: It took him two months to recover from the operation. 手术后，他过了两个月才康复。
2 [I] recover (from sth) to get back to normal again after a bad experience, etc 恢复正常: The old lady never really recovered from the shock of being mugged. 老太太遭抢劫受惊后，再也没有完全恢复过来。
3 [T] recover sth (from sb/sth) to find or get back sth that was lost or stolen 寻回，取回（遗失或失窃的物品）: Police recovered the stolen goods from a warehouse in South London. 警方在伦敦南部的一个仓库中寻回赃物。
4 [T] to get back the use of your senses, control of your emotions, etc 恢复知觉；（心情）平静下来

*recovery
/rɪˈkʌvəri ||; rɪˈkʌvərɪ/noun
1 [usu.sing] [U] recovery (from sth) a return to good health after an illness or to a normal state after a difficult period of time 康复；痊愈；恢复正常 [sing] to make a good/quick/speedy/slow recovery 康复得好╱快╱迅速╱慢 She's on the road to recovery (= getting better all the time) now. 她现正渐渐康复。 the prospects of economic recovery 经济复苏的展望
2 [U] recovery (of sth/sb) getting back sth that was lost, stolen or missing （遗失、失窃或失踪物品的）寻回，取回

recycle
/ˌri:ˈsaɪkl ||; riˈsaɪkḷ/verb[T]
1 to put used objects and materials through a process so that they can be used again 使循环再用；把废物处理再用；回收利用: recycled paper 再生纸 Aluminium cans can be recycled. 铝罐可以回收再用。
2 to keep used objects and materials and use them again 保留用过的物件再用；重复使用: Don't throw away your plastic carrier bags -- recycle them! 不要丢掉塑料购物袋─可以留下再用的！ ➔recyclable adj Most plastics are recyclable. 大部份塑料制品都可回收再用。

*red
/red ||; rɛd/noun [C,U] adj (redder;reddest)
1 (of) the colour of blood 红色（的）: red wine 红葡萄酒 She was dressed in red. 她身穿红色衣服。 ☞ We use crimson, maroon and scarlet to describe different shades of red. 不同的红色有crimson（深红色）、maroon（褐红色）及scarlet（猩红色）。
2 a colour that some people's faces become when they are embarrassed, angry, shy, etc （人的脸色因发窘、生气、腼腆等而）通红，发红: He went bright red when she spoke to him. 她跟他说话时，他满脸绯红。 to turn/be/go red in the face 脸变得通红
3 (used about a person's hair or an animal's fur) (of) a colour between red, orange and brown （指人的头发或动物的毛皮）褐红色（的）: She's got red hair and freckles. 她有一头褐红色的头发，一脸雀斑。
be in the red to have spent more money than you have in the bank, etc 出现赤字；负债；入不敷出: I'm £500 in the red at the moment. 我目前负债500英镑。 [OPP] be in the black 反义词为be in the black catch sb red-handed→CATCH¹ a red herring an idea or a subject which takes people's attention away from what is really important 分散注意力的事物 see red(informal 非正式) to become very angry 火冒三丈；很生气

*reduce
/rɪˈdju:s; US -ˈdu:s ||; rɪˈdus/verb[T]
1 reduce sth (from sth) (to sth);reduce sth (by sth) to make sth less or smaller in quantity, price, size, etc 减少，减低，减缩（数量、价钱、尺寸等）: The sign said ‘Reduce speed now’. 标志上写着“开始减速”。 [OPP] increase 反义词为increase
2 reduce sb/sth (from sth) to sth (often passive 常用于被动语态) to force sb/sth into a particular state or condition, usually a bad one 使处于某种（不佳的）状态: One of the older boys reduced the small child to tears. 其中一个年纪较大的男孩把那个小孩弄哭了。

*refer
/rɪˈfɜ:(r) ||; rɪˈfɝ/verb (referring;referred)
1 [I] refer to sb/sth (as sth) to mention or talk about sb/sth 提及；谈到；指: When he said ‘some students’, do you think he was referring to us? 当他说“一些学生”，你认为是在指我们吗？ She always referred to Ben as ‘that nice man’. 她老是把本称作“那个好心人”。
2 [I] refer to sb/sth to describe or be connected with sb/sth 形容；与…有关；指: The term ‘adolescent’ refers to young people between the ages of 12 and 17. “青少年”这个词指12至17岁的人。
3 [I] refer to sb/sth to find out information by asking sb or by looking in a book, etc 参考；查阅；查询；询问: If you don't understand a word you may refer to your dictionaries. 遇有不明白的词，可以翻查词典。
4 [T] refer sb/sth to sb/sth to send sb/sth to sb/sth else for help or to be dealt with 转送往某人或某处以便处理或寻求协助: The doctor has referred me to a specialist. 那位医生已把我转给一位专科医生诊治。

referee
/ˌrefəˈri: ||; ˌrɛfəˈri/noun[C]
1 (informal 非正式ref) the official person in sports such as football who controls the match and prevents players from breaking the rules （足球等的）裁判（员） A similar official in sports such as tennis is called an umpire. 网球等的裁判员叫做umpire。
2 (Brit 英) a person who gives information about your character and ability, usually in a letter, for example when you are hoping to be chosen for a job （为谋职者提供其性格、能力等证明的）介绍人，推荐人: Her teacher agreed to act as her referee. 她的老师答应当她的推荐人。 referee verb [I,T] Who refereed the match?

*reference
/ˈrefrəns ||; ˈrɛfrəns/noun
1 [C,U] (a) reference (to sb/sth) a written or spoken comment that mentions sb/sth 提及或谈到…的文字或言语: The article made a direct referenceto a certain member of the royal family. 文章直接提到某位王室成员。
2 [U] looking at sth for information 查阅；参考: The guidebook might be useful for future reference. 这本指南也许可作将来参考之用。
3 [C] a note, especially in a book, that tells you where certain information came from or can be found 参考书目；引文出处
4 [C] (abbr ref.) (used on business letters, etc) a special number that identifies a letter, etc （用于商业书信等）档案编号: Please quote our reference when replying. 回复时请注明我方档案编号。
5 [C] a statement or letter describing a person's character and ability that is given to a possible future employer （关于谋职者的性格、能力等的）介绍信，推荐信: My boss gave me a good reference. 我的上司为我写了一封不错的推荐信。
with reference to sb/sth(formal 正式) about or concerning sb/sth 有关；关于: I am writing with reference to your letter of 10 April... 本人谨此回复先生4月10日的来函…

ˈreference book

refine

refined
/rɪˈfaɪnd ||; rɪˈfaɪnd/adj
1 (used about a substance) that has been made pure by having other substances taken out of it （指物质）经过提炼的，去掉杂质的: refined sugar/oil/flour 精制糖；精炼的石油；精制面粉
2 (used about a person) polite; having very good manners （指人）优雅的，举止文雅的 [OPP] for senses 1 and 2 unrefined 第1及2义的反义词皆为unrefined
3 improved and therefore producing a better result 改进了的

refinement
/rɪˈfaɪnmənt ||; rɪˈfaɪnmənt/noun
1 [C] a small change that improves sth 细微的改良: The new model has electric windows and other refinements. 新型号有电动窗和其他改良装置。
2 [U] good manners and polite behaviour 优雅的举止

refinery
/rɪˈfaɪnəri ||; rɪˈfaɪnərɪ/noun [C] (plural refineries) a factory where a substance is made pure by having other substances taken out of it 提炼厂: an oil/sugar refinery 炼油厂；制糖厂

*reflect
/rɪˈflekt ||; rɪˈflɛkt/verb
1 [T] to send back light, heat or sound from a surface 反射（光、热或声音）: The windows reflected the bright morning sunlight. 窗子反射明亮的清晨阳光。
2 [T] reflect sb/sth (in sth) (usually passive 通常用于被动语态) to show an image of sb/sth on the surface of sth such as a mirror, water or glass 照出，映出，反映（某人或某物的影像）: She caught sight of herself reflected in the shop window. 她在商店橱窗里瞥见自己的影像。
3 [T] to show or express sth 反映；显示；表达: His music reflects his interest in African culture. 他的音乐显示出他对非洲文化的兴趣。
4 [I] reflect (on/upon sth) to think, especially deeply and carefully, about sth 仔细考虑；深思
reflect (well, badly, etc) on sb/sth to give a particular impression of sb/sth 影响某人或某事物的形象；给人某种印象: It reflects badly on the whole school if some of its pupils misbehave in public. 如果有些学生在公共场所行为不检，整个学校就会予人不良的印象。

*reflection
/rɪˈflekʃn ||; rɪˈflɛkʃən/ (brit also 英亦作 reflexion) noun
1 [C] an image that you see in a mirror, in water or on a shiny surface （镜中、水中或光亮表面的）映像，倒影: He admired his reflection in the mirror. 他欣赏自己在镜中的映像。
2 [U] the sending back of light, heat or sound from a surface （光、热或声音的）反射
3 [C] a thing that shows what sb/sth is like 反映某人或某事物的东西: Your clothes are a reflection of your personality. 衣着反映个性。
4 [sing] a reflection on/upon sb/sth something that causes people to form a good or bad opinion about sb/sth 影响…形象的事物: Parents often feel that their children's behaviour is a reflection on themselves. 父母往往觉得子女的行为会影响他们的声誉。
5 [U] [C] careful thought about sth 深思: a book of his reflections on fatherhood 一本关于他对身为人父的看法的书
on reflection after thinking again 经过重新考虑: I think, on reflection, that we were wrong. 经过再三考虑之后，我认为我们错了。

reflective
/rɪˈflektɪv ||; rɪˈflɛktɪv/adj
1 (written 书面语) (used about a person, mood, etc) thinking deeply about things （指人、心理活动等）深思熟虑的，沉思的: a reflective expression 沉思的表情
2 (used about a surface) sending back light or heat （指物体的表面）反射光或热的: Wear reflective strips when you're cycling at night. 在夜间骑自行车要佩戴反光片。
3 reflective (of sth) showing what sth is like 反映出…的

reflector
/rɪˈflektə(r) ||; rɪˈflɛktɚ/noun[C]
1 a surface that sends back (reflects) light, heat or sound that hits it 反射器；反射体
2 a small piece of glass or plastic on a bicycle or on clothing that can be seen at night when light shines on it （自行车上的）反光镜；（衣服上的）反光片

reflex
/ˈri:fleks ||; ˈriflɛks/noun
1 [C] (also reflex action) a sudden movement or action that you make without thinking 反射作用；本能反应: She put her hands out as a reflex to stop her fall. 她凭本能反应伸出双手，以防跌倒。
2 reflexes [pl] the ability to act quickly when necessary 反应能力: A good tennis player needs to have excellent reflexes. 出色的网球员需要有极佳的反应能力。

ˌreflex ˈangle
noun [C] (mathematics数学) an angle of more than 180° 优角（大于180度的角） ☞Compare acute angle, obtuse angle and right angle. 与acute angle、obtuse angle及right angle比较。 ☞picture at angle 见angle插图

reflexion
(Brit 英) =REFLECTION

reflexive
/rɪˈfleksɪv ||; rɪˈflɛksɪv/adj noun [C] (grammar语法) (a word or verb form) showing that the person who performs an action is also affected by it 受自身动作影响的，反身的（词或动词形式）: In ‘He cut himself’, ‘cut’ is a reflexive verb and ‘himself’ is a reflexive pronoun. He cut himself一句中，cut是反身动词，himself是反身代词。

*reform
/rɪˈfɔ:m ||; rɪˈfɔrm/verb
1 [T] to change a system, the law, etc in order to make it better 改革，改良（制度、法律等）: to reform the examination system 改革考试制度
2 [I,T] to improve your behaviour; to make sb do this （使）改过自新 · Our prisons aim to reform criminals, not simply to punish them. 我们设立监狱的目的在使罪犯改过自新，而非只是要惩罚他们。 reform noun [C,U]

reformation
/ˌrefəˈmeɪʃn ||; ˌrɛfɚˈmeʃən/noun

*regard¹
/rɪˈgɑ:d ||; rɪˈgɑrd/verb[T]
1 regard sb/sth as sth;regard sb/sth (with sth) to think of sb/sth (in the way mentioned) 把…看作；认为；视为: Do you regard this issue as important? 你认为这个问题重要吗？ Her work is highly regarded (= people have a high opinion of it). 她的工作得到高度评价。 In some villages newcomers are regarded with suspicion. 在一些村庄里，新来的人会受到怀疑。
2 (formal 正式) to look at sb/sth for a while 凝视
as regards sb/sth(formal 正式) in connection with sb/sth 有关；关于: What are your views as regards this proposal? 你对这个提议有什么看法？
regard²
/rɪˈgɑ:d ||; rɪˈgɑrd/noun
1 [U] regard to/for sb/sth attention to or care for sb/sth 注意；关心: He shows little regard for other people's feelings. 他不太关心别人的感受。
2 [U] [sing] (a) regard (for sb/sth) a feeling of admiration for sb/sth: respect 钦佩；赞赏；敬重；尊敬: She obviously has great regardfor your ability. 她显然很赞赏你的能力。
3 regards [pl] (used especially to end a letter politely) kind thoughts; best wishes （尤用于书信结尾的客套话）致意，问候: Please give my regards to your parents. 请代我问候你的双亲。
in/with regard to sb/sth;in this/that/one regard(formal 正式) about sb/sth; connected with sb/sth 关于；在…方面: With regard to the details -- these will be finalized later. 至于细节，稍后就会定案。

*region
/ˈri:dʒən ||; ˈridʒən/noun[C]
1 a part of the country or the world; a large area of land （国家或世界的）地区，区域，地带: desert/tropical/polar regions 沙漠╱热带╱南北极地区 This region of France is very mountainous. 法国的这一地区多山。 ☞ Look at the note at district. 参看district的注释。

*register¹
/ˈredʒɪstə(r) ||; ˈrɛdʒɪstɚ/verb
1 [I,T] to put a name on an official list 登记；注册: You should register with a doctor nearby. 你应向附近的医生办理登记。 All births, deaths and marriages must be registered. 所有出生、死亡及结婚事项都必须注册。
2 [I,T] to show sth or to be shown on a measuring instrument （在测量仪器上）显示 · The thermometer registered 32°C. 温度计显示出32摄氏度。 The earthquake registered 6.4 on the Richter scale. 这次地震为里氏6.4级。
3 [T] to show feelings, opinions, etc 表露，表达（感受、意见等）: Her face registered intense dislike. 她脸上露出非常憎恶的神色。
4 [I,T] (often used in negative sentences 常用于否定句) to notice sth and remember it; to be noticed and remembered （被）注意到；（被）记住: He told me his name but it didn't register. 他告诉过我他的名字，但我没有记住。
5 [T] to send a letter or package by special (registered) post 以挂号方式邮寄
*register²
/ˈredʒɪstə(r) ||; ˈrɛdʒɪstɚ/noun
1 [C] an official list of names, etc or a book that contains this kind of list 正式的名单；名册；登记簿: The teacher calls the register first thing in the morning. 老师早上首先做的就是点名。 the electoral register (= of people who are able to vote in an election) 选民名册
2 [C,U] the type of language (formal or informal) that is used in a piece of writing 语域

ˌregistered ˈpost
noun [U] (Brit 英) a way of sending things by post that you pay extra for. If your letter or package is lost the post office will make a payment to you. 挂号邮寄（须付额外费用，邮件如有遗失，由邮局负责赔偿）

*regret¹
/rɪˈgret ||; rɪˈgrɛt/verb [T] (regretting;regretted)
1 to feel sorry that you did sth or that you did not do sth 感到遗憾、惋惜、后悔或懊悔: I hope you won't regret your decision later. 我希望你以后不会后悔作出这决定。 Do you regret not taking the job? 你没有接受那份工作，感到后悔吗？
2 (formal 正式) used as a way of saying that you are sorry for sth （用于表示抱歉）: I regret to inform you that your application has been unsuccessful. 很抱歉通知你，你的申请没有成功。
*regret²

regrettable
/rɪˈgretəbl ||; rɪˈgrɛtəbḷ/adj that you should feel sorry or sad about 令人遗憾、惋惜或懊悔的: It is regrettable that the police were not informed sooner. 警方没有早一点获通报，这是令人遗憾的。 ➔regrettably /-əbli ||; -əblɪ/ adv Regrettably, most hotels are not well-equipped for disabled people.

regroup
/ˌri:ˈgru:p ||; riˈgrup/verb
1 [I,T] regroup (sth) (for sth) to arrange the way people or soldiers work together in a new way, especially in order to continue fighting or attacking sb 重组；重新编组: They regrouped their forces and renewed the attack. 他们重新聚集兵力，再次发动进攻。 After its election defeat, the party needs to regroup. 选举失败后，该党需要重组。
2 [I] (used about a person) to return to a normal state after an unpleasant experience or a period of difficulty, and become ready to make an effort again with new enthusiasm or strength ﹙人在经历不幸或困难后﹚恢复元气: Summer is a time to relax, regroup and catch up on all those things you've been putting off all year. 你可以利用夏天放松自己、恢复元气以及做你一年来一直拖着未干的所有事情。

*regular¹
/ˈregjələ(r) ||; ˈrɛgjəlɚ/adj
1 having the same amount of space or time between each thing or part 均匀的；有规律的；按时的: a regular heartbeat 均匀的心跳 Nurses checked her blood pressure at regular intervals. 护士每隔一定的时间给她量血压。 The fire alarms are tested on a regular basis. 火警警报器都会定期检测。 We have regular meetings every Thursday. 我们每星期四举行例会。 [OPP] irregular 反义词为irregular
2 done or happening often 经常做或发生: The doctor advised me to take regular exercise. 医生建议我经常运动。 Accidents are a regular occurrence on this road. 这条路经常出事。
3 going somewhere or doing sth often 经常去某地或做某事的: a regular customer 老主顾 We're regular visitors to Britain. 我们是英国的常客。
4 normal or usual 正常的；通常的: Who is your regular dentist? 你通常找哪个牙医看牙齿？
5 not having any individual part that is different from the rest 整齐的；匀称的: regular teeth/features 整齐的牙齿；端正的五官 a regular pattern 匀称的图案 [OPP] irregular 反义词为irregular
6 fixed or permanent 固定的；常备的: a regular income/job 固定收入╱工作 a regular soldier/army 常备兵；正规军
7 (especially US 尤为美) standard, average or normal 标准的；普通的: Regular or large fries? 炸马铃薯条要普通的还是大包的？
8 (grammar语法) (used about a noun, verb, etc) having the usual or expected plural, verb form, etc （指名词、动词等）按规则变化的: ‘Walk’ is a regular verb. walk是规则动词。 [OPP] irregular 反义词为irregular ➔regularly adv to have a car serviced regularly 定期把汽车送去检修 ➔regularity /ˌregjuˈlærəti ||; ˌrɛgjəˈlærətɪ/ noun [U] [C]: My car breaks down with increasing regularity. 我的汽车越来越频繁地抛锚。
regular²
/ˈregjələ(r) ||; ˈrɛgjəlɚ/noun[C]
1 (informal 非正式) a person who goes to a particular shop, bar, restaurant, etc very often 老主顾；常客
2 a person who usually does a particular activity or sport 通常做某种活动或运动的人
3 a permanent member of the army, navy, etc 正规军人；常备兵

regulate
/ˈregjuleɪt ||; ˈrɛgjəˌlet/verb[T]
1 to control sth by using laws or rules （用法律或规则）管制，管理
2 to control a machine, piece of equipment, etc 控制（机器、设备等）；调节: You can regulate the temperature in the car with this dial. 汽车里的温度可以用这个刻度盘来调节。

*regulation
/ˌregjuˈleɪʃn ||; ˌrɛgjəˈleʃən/noun
1 [C] [usu.pl] an official rule that controls how sth is done 法规；条例；规则；规定: to observe/obey the safety regulations 遵守╱遵从安全规则 The plans must comply with EU regulations. 那些计划必须符合欧洲联盟的规定。
2 [U] the control of sth by using rules （以规则）管理，管制，控制: state regulation of imports and exports 国家对进出口的管理

regurgitate
/rɪˈgɜ:dʒɪteɪt ||; riˈgɝdʒəˌtet/verb[T]
1 (formal 正式) to bring food that has been swallowed back up into the mouth again 反胃吐出（食物）: The bird regurgitates half-digested fish to feed its young. 那鸟以反胃吐出的半消化了的鱼喂小鸟。
2 to repeat sth you have heard or read without really thinking about it or understanding it （未理解而）机械地重复: He's just regurgitating what his father says. 他只是机械地重复他父亲的话。

rehabilitate
/ˌri:əˈbɪlɪteɪt ||; ˌriəˈbɪləˌtet/verb [T] to help sb to live a normal life again after an illness, being in prison, etc 使（病愈、出狱等后）重过正常生活；使康复 ➔rehabilitation /ˌri:əˌbɪlɪˈteɪʃn ||; ˌriəˌbɪləˈteʃən/ noun [U]: a rehabilitation centre for drug addicts 吸毒者康复中心

rehearsal
/rɪˈhɜ:sl ||; rɪˈhɝsḷ/noun [C,U] the time when you practise a play, dance, piece of music, etc before you perform it to other people （戏剧、舞蹈、音乐等的）排练，排演，彩排: a dress rehearsal (= when all the actors wear their stage clothes) 彩排（正式演出前的化装排演） ➔rehearse /rɪˈhɜ:s ||; rɪˈhɝs/ verb [I,T] rehearse (for sth)

reheat
/ˌri:ˈhi:t ||; riˈhit/verb [T] to heat cooked food again after it has been left to go cold 重新加热﹙食物﹚

reign
/reɪn ||; ren/verb[I]
1 reign (over sb/sth) (used about a king or queen) to rule a country （指国王或女王）统治，当政 (figurative 比喻) the reigning world champion 目前的世界冠军
2 reign (over sb/sth) to be in charge of a business or an organization 主管（企业或组织）
3 to be present as the most important quality of a particular situation 支配；占重要位置: Chaos reigned after the first snow of the winter. 冬季初雪后，到处一片混乱。 ➔reign noun [C]

reimburse
/ˌri:ɪmˈbɜ:s ||; ˌriɪmˈbɝs/verb [T] (formal 正式) to pay money back to sb 付还；赔偿: The company will reimburse you in full for your travelling expenses. 公司会为你报销全部出差费。

rein
/reɪn ||; ren/noun [C] [usu.pl] a long thin piece of leather that is held by the rider and used to control a horse's movements （控制马匹的）缰绳 ☞picture at horse 见horse插图

reincarnation
/ˌri:ɪnkɑ:ˈneɪʃn ||; ˌriɪnkɑrˈneʃən/noun
1 [U] the belief that people who have died can live again in a different body 轮回转世说（认为人死后会以不同的肉体再生）: Do you believe in reincarnation? 你相信轮回转世说吗？
2 [C] a person or animal whose body is believed to contain the soul of a dead person 死人投胎的人或动物；转世化身: He believes he is the reincarnation of an Egyptian princess. 他认为自己是一位埃及公主的再生。 ☞Look at incarnation. 参看incarnation。

reindeer
/ˈreɪndɪə(r) ||; ˈrenˌdɪr/noun [C] (plural reindeer) a type of large brownish wild animal that eats grass and lives in Arctic regions 驯鹿（栖息在北极地区）

reinforce
/ˌri:ɪnˈfɔ:s ||; ˌriɪnˈfɔrs/verb [T] to make sth stronger 增强；加强；巩固；强化: Concrete can be reinforced with steel bars. 混凝土可以钢筋加固。

reinforcement
/ˌri:ɪnˈfɔ:smənt ||; ˌriɪnˈfɔrsmənt/noun
1 [U] making sth stronger 增强；加强；强化: The sea wall is weak in places and needs reinforcement. 海堤有些地方不太牢靠，须要加固。
2 reinforcements [pl] extra people who are sent to make an army, navy, etc stronger 援兵；援军；增援部队

reinstate
/ˌri:ɪnˈsteɪt ||; ˌriɪnˈstet/verb[T]
1 reinstate sb (in/as sth) to give back a job or position that was taken from sb 使恢复原职: He was cleared of the charge of theft and reinstated as Head of Security. 他已洗脱盗窃的指控，恢复了安全部主任的职务。
2 to return sth to its former position or role 使恢复原状或原位 ➔reinstatement noun [U]

reinvent
/ˌri:ɪnˈvent ||; ˌriɪnˈvɛnt/verb [T] reinvent the wheel to waste time creating sth that already exists and works well 无谓地重复；浪费时间做无用功

*reject¹
/rɪˈdʒekt ||; rɪˈdʒɛkt/verb [T] to refuse to accept sb/sth 拒绝接受: The plan was rejected as being impractical. 计划因不切实际而遭否决。 ➔rejection noun [C,U] Gargi got a rejection from Leeds University. 加吉申请就读利兹大学未被录取。 There has been total rejection of the new policy. 人们完全不接受那项新政策。
reject²
/ˈri:dʒekt ||; ˈridʒɛkt/noun [C] a person or thing that is not accepted because he/she/it is not good enough 因未符合要求而被拒绝的人或物: Rejects are sold at half price. 次品以半价出售。

rejoice
/rɪˈdʒɔɪs ||; rɪˈdʒɔɪs/verb [I] (formal 正式)rejoice (at/over sth) to feel or show great happiness 欢欣；欢腾 ➔rejoicing noun [U]: There were scenes of rejoicing when the war ended. 战争结束时人们欢欣鼓舞。

rejoin
/ˌri:ˈdʒɔɪn ||; ˌriˈdʒɔɪn/verb [T] [I] to join sb/sth again after leaving him/her/it 重新回到…身边

rejuvenate
/rɪˈdʒu:vəneɪt ||; rɪˈdʒuvəˌnet/verb [T] (often passive 常用于被动语态) to make sb/sth feel or look younger 使感觉或看来较年轻；使恢复活力 ➔rejuvenation /rɪˌdʒu:vəˈneɪʃn ||; rɪˌdʒuvəˈneʃən/ noun [U]

rekindle
/ˌri:ˈkɪndl ||; riˈkɪndḷ/verb [T] (written 书面语) to make sth become active again 使重新活跃；使复苏: to rekindle feelings/hopes/interest/memories 再次唤起情感；重新点燃希望之火；恢复兴趣/记忆

relapse
/rɪˈlæps ||; rɪˈlæps/verb [I] to become worse again after an improvement （改善后）再恶化；故态复萌: to relapse into bad habits 再染恶习 relapse /ˈri:læps ||; ˈrilæps/ noun [C]: The patient had a relapse and then died. 病人旧病复发后不久就去世了。

*relate
/rɪˈleɪt ||; rɪˈlet/verb[T]
1 relate A to/with B to show or make a connection between two or more things 显示…与…有关；使有关联: The report relates heart disease to high levels of stress. 这报告显示心脏病与精神压力过重有关。
2 (formal 正式)relate sth (to sb) to tell a story to sb 讲述；叙述: He related his side of the story to a journalist. 他向记者讲述了他就这件事所知道的情况。
relate to sb/sth
1 to be concerned or involved with sth 与某人或某事物有关
2 to be able to understand how sb feels 领略或理解别人的感受: Some teenagers find it hard to relate to their parents. 有些青年人觉得很难理解父母。

related
/rɪˈleɪtɪd ||; rɪˈletɪd/adj related (to sb/sth)
1 connected with sb/sth 与…有关或相关的: The rise in the cost of living is directly related to the price of oil. 生活费上升与油价直接有关。
2 of the same family 有亲属关系的；属于同一家族的: We are related by marriage. 我们有姻亲关系。

*relation
/rɪˈleɪʃn ||; rɪˈleʃən/noun
1 relations [pl] relations (with sb);relations (between A and B) the way that people, groups, countries, etc feel about or behave towards each other （国家、群体、人际等的）关系: The police officer stressed that good relations with the community were essential. 那位警官强调，与区内的人维持良好关系是十分重要的。
2 [U] relation (between sth and sth);relation (to sth) the connection between two or more things （两个或以上事物之间的）关系，关联: There seems to be little relation between the cost of the houses and their size. 房子的价格与大小似乎没有关系。 Their salaries bear no relation to the number of hours they work. 他们的薪金与工作时间长短没有关系。
3 [C] a member of your family 亲戚；亲属: a close/distant relation 近亲；远亲 [SYN] relative 同义词为relative ☞You can use the expressions: ‘What relation are you to each other?’ and ‘Are you any relation to each other?’ 注意以下两种不同说法：‘What relation are you to each other?’“你们有什么亲属关系？”及‘Are you any relation to each other?’“你们是亲戚吗？”
in/with relation to sb/sth
1 concerning sb/sth 关于；有关；涉及: Many questions were asked, particularly in relation to the cost of the new buildings. 大家提出了很多问题，尤其是涉及新楼的成本。
2 compared with 与…相比: Prices are low in relation to those in other parts of Europe. 与欧洲其他地方相比，物价是较低的。

*relationship
/rɪˈleɪʃnʃɪp ||; rɪˈleʃənˌʃɪp/noun[C]
1 a relationship (with sb/sth);a relationship (between A and B) the way that people, groups, countries, etc feel about or behave towards each other （人际、群体、国家等的）关系: The relationship between the parents and the school has improved greatly. 家长与校方的关系已大大改善。
2 a relationship (with sb);a relationship (between A and B) a friendly or loving connection between people 友谊；友情；爱情；恋情: to have a relationship with sb 与某人谈恋爱 He'd never been in a serious relationshipbefore he got married. 他结婚以前从来没有认真谈过恋爱。 The film describes the relationship between a young man and an older woman. 影片描述一个年轻男子与一个年纪较大的女子的恋情。 Do you have a close relationship with your brother? 你跟你的哥哥关系密切吗？
3 a relationship (to sth);a relationship (between A and B) the way in which two or more things are connected （两样或以上事物的）关系，关联: Is there a relationship between violence on TV and the increase in crime? 电视上的暴力与罪案增加有关系吗？
4 a relationship (to sb);a relationship (between A and B) a family connection 亲属或亲戚关系: ‘What is your relationship to Bruce?’ ‘He's married to my cousin.’ “你与布鲁斯有什么亲属关系？”“他是我表妹的丈夫。”

*relative¹
/ˈrelətɪv ||; ˈrɛlətɪv/adj
1 relative (to sth) when compared to sb/sth else 与…相比的；比较上的；相对的: the position of the earth relative to the sun 地球相对于太阳的位置 They live in relative luxury. 他们的生活过得比较奢华。
2 (grammar语法) referring to an earlier noun, sentence or part of a sentence 与前述名词、短语或句子相关联的；表示关系的: In the phrase ‘the lady who lives next door’, ‘who’ is a relative pronoun and ‘who lives next door’ is a relative clause. 在the lady who lives next door这个短语中，who是关系代词，who lives next door是关系从句。 For more information about relative pronouns and clauses, look at the Quick Grammar Reference section at the back of this dictionary. 有关关系代词和关系从句的详细用法，参看本词典末“语法便览”部份。
*relative²
/ˈrelətɪv ||; ˈrɛlətɪv/noun [C] a member of your family 亲戚；亲属: a close/distant relative 近亲；远亲 [SYN] relation 同义词为relation

relatively
/ˈrelətɪvli ||; ˈrɛlətɪvlɪ/adv to quite a large degree, especially when compared to others 很大程度上，相当（尤指与他物比较时）: Spanish is a relatively easy language to learn. 西班牙语是一种颇好学的语言。

relativity
/ˌreləˈtɪvəti ||; ˌrɛləˈtɪvətɪ/noun [U] (in physics 物理学) Einstein's belief that all movement is affected by space, light, time and GRAVITY(= the force that makes things fall to the ground) 相对论（指爱因斯坦的理论，认为所有运动都受空间、光、时间及引力的影响）

*relax
/rɪˈlæks ||; rɪˈlæks/verb
1 [I] to rest while you are doing sth enjoyable, especially after work or effort 休息（尤指在工作或努力之后）: This holiday will give you a chance to relax. 这个假期会让你有机会轻松一下。 They spent the evening relaxing in front of the television. 他们这一晚在电视机前轻松度过。
2 [I] to become calmer and less worried 变得镇定或放心: Relax -- everything's going to be OK! 放心好了，一切都不会有问题的！
3 [I,T] to become or make sb/sth become less hard or tight （使）放松，松弛 · A hot bath will relax you after a hard day's work. 经过一天辛劳工作，洗个热水浴会使你轻松舒畅。 Don't relax your grip on the rope! 抓紧绳子别松手！
4 [T] to make rules or laws less strict 放宽（规则或法律）

*relaxation
/ˌri:lækˈseɪʃn ||; ˌrilæksˈeʃən/noun
1 [C,U] something that you do in order to rest, especially after work or effort 娱乐；消遣: Everyone needs time for rest and relaxation. 人人都需要有休息和娱乐的时间。
2 [U] making sth less strict, tight or strong 松弛；放松；放宽

*relaxed
/rɪˈlækst ||; rɪˈlækst/adj not worried or tense 不忧虑的；不紧张的；轻松的: The relaxed atmosphere made everyone feel at ease. 轻松的气氛使大家都感到自在。

relaxing
/rɪˈlæksɪŋ ||; rɪˈlæksɪŋ/adj pleasant, helping you to rest and become less worried 令人舒服的；使人轻松的: a quiet relaxing holiday 一个安静惬意的假期

relay¹
/rɪˈleɪ;ˈri:leɪ ||; rɪˈle; ˈrile/verb [T] (past tense past participle relayed)
1 to receive and then pass on a signal or message 转递（信号或信息）: Instructions were relayed to us by phone. 指示是通过电话传给我们的。
2 (Brit 英) to put a programme on the radio or television 广播，播放，转播（电台或电视节目）
relay²
/ˈri:leɪ ||; ˈrile/ (also relay race) noun [C] a race in which each member of a team runs, swims, etc one part of the race 接力赛

*release¹
/rɪˈli:s ||; rɪˈlis/verb[T]
1 release sb/sth (from sth) to allow sb/sth to be free 释放；使自由: He's been released from prison. 他已获释出狱。 (figurative 比喻) His firm released him for two days a week to go on a training course. 公司准许他每周离开两天去参加一个培训班。
2 to stop holding sth so that it can move, fly, fall, etc freely 放开；松开: 1000 balloons were released at the ceremony. 仪式上放了1000个气球。 (figurative 比喻) Crying is a good way to release pent-up emotions. 哭是发泄积郁的好办法。
3 to move sth from a fixed position （把某物）从固定位置移开: He released the handbrake and drove off. 他松开手剎车，驱车而去。
4 to allow sth to be known by the public 公开；发布；发表: The identity of the victim has not been released. 受害者的身分还没有公布。
5 to make a film, record, etc available so the public can see or hear it 发行（影片、唱片等）: Their new single is due to be released next week. 他们的新单曲唱片定于下周发行。
*release²
/rɪˈli:s ||; rɪˈlis/noun[C,U]
1 (a) release (of sth) (from sth) the freeing of sth or the state of being freed 释放；获释: The release of the hostages took place this morning. 人质是在今晨获释的。 I had a great feeling of release when my exams were finished. 考试结束使我如释重负。
2 a book, film, record, piece of news, etc that has been made available to the public; the act of making sth available to the public 发行的新书、电影或唱片；发布的新闻；发行；发布: a press release 新闻稿 The band played their latest release. 该乐队演奏他们最新发行的唱片歌曲。 The film won't be/go on release until March. 这部电影要到三月才会发行。

relegate
/ˈrelɪgeɪt ||; ˈrɛləˌget/verb [T] to put sb/sth into a lower level or position 把﹙某人╱某事物﹚降级╱置于较次要位置: The team finished bottom and were relegated to the second division. 这支球队最后积分垫底，被降至乙组。 ➔relegation /ˌrelɪˈgeɪʃn ||; ˌrɛləˈgeʃən/ noun [U]

relent
/rɪˈlent ||; rɪˈlɛnt/verb[I]
1 to finally agree to sth that you had refused 松口；变得宽容: Her parents finally relented and allowed her to go to the concert. 她父母最后松口，准许她去听音乐会。
2 to become less determined, strong, etc 减弱；缓和: The heavy rain finally relented and we went out. 大雨终于减弱，我们出去了。

relentless
/rɪˈlentləs ||; rɪˈlɛntlɪs/adj not stopping or changing 不间断的；无情的: the relentless fight against crime 不间断地与犯罪作斗争 ➔relentlessly adv The sun beat down relentlessly. 烈日无情地曝晒着。

*relevant
/ˈreləvənt ||; ˈrɛləvənt/adj relevant (to sb/sth)
1 connected with what is happening or being talked about 有关的；切题的: Much of what was said was not directly relevant to my case. 所说的内容大部份都与我的情况没有直接关联。
2 important and useful 重要且有用的: Many people feel that poetry is no longer relevant in today's world. 很多人认为在现今的世界中，诗歌已经无关重要。 [OPP] irrelevant 反义词为irrelevant ➔relevance noun [U]: I honestly can't see the relevance of what he said. 我实在看不出他所说的话有什么意义。

*reliable
/rɪˈlaɪəbl ||; rɪˈlaɪəbḷ/adj that you can trust 值得信赖的；可靠的: Japanese cars are usually very reliable. 日本汽车质量一般都很可靠。 Is he a reliable witness? 他是个值得信赖的证人吗？ [OPP] unreliable 反义词为unreliable ☞verb rely 动词为rely ➔reliability /rɪˌlaɪəˈbɪləti ||; rɪˌlaɪəˈbɪlətɪ/ noun [U] ➔reliably /-əbli ||; -əblɪ/ adv I have been reliably informed that there will be no trains tomorrow. 我获得可靠消息说明天火车停开。

reliance
/rɪˈlaɪəns ||; rɪˈlaɪəns/noun [U] reliance on sb/sth
1 being able to trust sb/sth 信任；信赖: Don't place too much relianceon her promises. 不要太相信她的承诺。
2 not being able to live or work without sb/sth; being dependent on sb/sth 依赖；依靠 ☞verb rely 动词为rely

reliant
/rɪˈlaɪənt ||; rɪˈlaɪənt/adj reliant on sb/sth not being able to live or work without sb/sth 依赖；依靠: They are totally reliant on the state for financial support. 他们完全依靠国家的财政支持。 ☞verb rely 动词为rely ☞ Look at self-reliant. 参看self-reliant。

relic

*relief
/rɪˈli:f ||; rɪˈlif/noun
1 [U] [sing] relief (from sth) the feeling that you have when sth unpleasant stops or becomes less strong （不愉快感受的）解除，缓和 [sing] What a relief! That awful noise has stopped. 真叫人松了一口气！那讨厌的声音停了。 [sing] It was a great relief to know they were safe. 知道他们平安无事，我觉得很安慰。 to breathe a sigh of relief 松一口气 To my relief, he didn't argue with my suggestion at all. 令我欣慰的是，他没有反驳我的建议。
2 [U] the removal or reduction of pain, worry, etc （痛楚、忧虑等的）消除，减轻: These tablets provide pain relief for up to four hours. 这些药片能缓和疼痛达四个小时。
3 [U] money or food that is given to help people who are in trouble or difficulty 救济物品或物资；救济金: disaster relief for the flood victims 为水灾灾民提供的赈济物资
4 [U] a reduction in the amount of tax you have to pay 税款减免

relieve
/rɪˈli:v ||; rɪˈliv/verb [T] to make an unpleasant feeling or situation stop or get better 解除，舒缓（痛苦、困境）: This injection should relieve the pain. 这一针应可减轻疼痛。 We played cards to relieve the boredom. 我们玩纸牌消遣。 relieve sb of sth(formal 正式) to take sth away from sb 从某人身上取去某物: to relieve sb of responsibility 免除某人的责任

*relieved
/rɪˈli:vd ||; rɪˈlivd/adj pleased because your fear or worry has been taken away 宽心的；宽慰的: I was very relieved to hear that you weren't seriously hurt. 听说你伤势不重，我感到很宽慰。

*religion

2 [C] one of the systems of beliefs that is based on a belief in a god or gods 宗教: the Christian/Hindu/Muslim/Sikh religion 基督教；印度教；伊斯兰教；锡克教

*religious
/rɪˈlɪdʒəs ||; rɪˈlɪdʒəs/adj

*rely
/rɪˈlaɪ ||; rɪˈlaɪ/verb [I] (present participle relying third person singular present relies;past tense past participle relied)rely on/upon sb/sth (to do sth)
1 to need sb/sth and not be able to live or work properly without him/her/it 依赖；依靠: The old lady had to rely on other people to do her shopping for her. 那位老太太得靠别人替她购物。
2 to trust sb/sth to work or behave well 信赖；信任；指望: Can I rely on you to keep a secret? 我可以指望你为我保守秘密吗？ ☞noun reliance 名词为reliance ☞Look at reliable and reliant. 参看reliable及reliant。

*remain
/rɪˈmeɪn ||; rɪˈmen/verb
1 linking verb to stay or continue in the same place or condition 逗留，停留（在某地或某状况）；保持不变: to remain silent/standing/seated 保持沉默；继续站着；继续坐着 Josef went to live in America but his family remained behind in Europe. 约瑟夫到美国居住，但他的家人仍然留在欧洲。
2 [I] to be left after other people or things have gone 剩下；余下；剩余: They spent the two remaining days of their holidays buying presents to take home. 他们利用剩下的两天假期买带回家的礼物。
3 [I] to still need to be done, said or dealt with 留待，尚待（做、说或处理）: It remains to be seen (= we do not know yet)whether we've made the right decision. 我们做出的这个决定正确与否尚待观察。 Although he seems very pleasant, the fact remains that I don't trust him. 虽然他这个人似乎很讨人喜欢，但我仍然不信任他。

remainder
/rɪˈmeɪndə(r) ||; rɪˈmendɚ/noun[sing] [with.sop] usuallythe remainder the people, things, etc that are left after the others have gone away or been dealt with; the rest 剩余、余下或其余的人或物

remains
/rɪˈmeɪnz ||; rɪˈmenz/noun[pl]
1 what is left behind after other parts have been used or taken away 剩下或剩余的部份: The builders found the remains of a Roman mosaic floor. 建筑工人发现了一处有古罗马式拼花地板的遗迹。
2 (formal 正式) a dead body (sometimes one that has been found somewhere a long time after death) 遗体；遗骨: Human remains were discovered in the wood. 树林内发现人类骸骨。

/ˈremədi ||; ˈrɛmədɪ/noun [C] (plural remedies)a remedy (for sth)
1 something that makes you better when you are ill or in pain 治疗；治疗法；药物: Hot lemon with honey is a good remedy for colds. 热柠檬水加蜂蜜是治疗伤风的良药。

*remember
/rɪˈmembə(r) ||; rɪˈmɛmbɚ/verb[I,T]
1 remember (sb/sth);remember (doing sth);remember that... to have sb/sth in your mind or to bring sb/sth back into your mind 记得；想起: We arranged to go out tonight -- remember? 我们今晚计划要外出─还记得吗？ As far as I can remember, I haven't seen him before. 根据我的记忆，我以前没有见过他。 I'm sorry. I don't remember your name. 很抱歉，我记不起你的名字。 Do you remember the night we first met? 你记得我们初相识的那个晚上吗？ Remember that we're having visitors tonight. 记住今晚我们有客人来。 Can you remember when we bought the stereo? 你记得我们是什么时候买的音响吗？
2 remember (sth/to do sth) to not forget to do what you have to do 记住；不忘记: I remembered to buy the coffee. 我记得买咖啡。 Remember to turn the lights off before you leave. 离开以前不要忘记关灯。
Notice that if you remember to do something, you don't forget to do it. If you remember doing something, you have a picture or memory in your mind of doing it I remember leaving my keys on the table last night. Remember to take your keys when you go out. remember to dosomething表示记得／没有忘记做某事。remember doing something是指记忆起曾做过某事：I remember leaving my keys on the table last night.我记得昨晚把钥匙放在桌子上的。·Remember to take your keys when you go out.出门的时候不要忘记带钥匙。
3 [T] to give money, etc to sb/sth 给，赠（钱等）: to remember sb in your will 在遗嘱里给某人留下遗赠
4 (formal 正式) to think about and show respect for sb who is dead 纪念（死者）
remember me to sb used when you want to send good wishes to a person you have not seen for a long time （代为问候某人）: Please remember me to your wife. 请代我问候你的太太。 ☞Look at the note at remind. 参看remind的注释。

remembrance
/rɪˈmembrəns ||; rɪˈmɛmbrəns/noun [U] (formal 正式) thinking about and showing respect for sb who is dead 纪念；怀念: a service in remembrance of those killed in the war 纪念战争死难者的仪式

*remind
/rɪˈmaɪnd ||; rɪˈmaɪnd/verb[T]
1 remind sb (about/of sth);remind sb (to do sth/that...) to help sb to remember sth, especially sth important that he/she has to do 提醒（尤指必须做的要事）: Can you remind me of your address? 能否提醒我一下你的地址？ He reminded the children to wash their hands. 他提醒孩子们要洗手。 Remind me what we're supposed to be doing tomorrow. 提醒我一下我们明天该做的事。
2 remind sb of sb/sth to cause sb to remember sb/sth 使回想起: That smell reminds me of school. 那种气味使我想起学校生活。 You remind me of your father. 你使我想起你的父亲。 ☞ You remember something by yourself. If somebody or something reminds you of something he/she/it causes you to remember it Did you remember to phone Ali last night? Remind me to phone Ali later. 自己记起就说remember，若别人或某事物令你记起就用remind：Did you remember to phone Ali last night? 你昨晚有没有记得给阿里打电话？·Remind me to phone Ali later.过一会儿提醒我给阿里打电话。

reminiscent
/ˌremɪˈnɪsnt ||; ˌrɛməˈnɪsṇt/adj (not before a noun 不用于名词前) that makes you remember sb/sth; similar to 怀旧；使想起某人或某事物；相似: His suit was reminiscent of an old army uniform. 他这套衣服与过去一种军装很相似。

remote
/rɪˈməʊt ||; rɪˈmot/adj
1 remote (from sth) far away from where other people live 边远的；偏僻的: a remote island in the Pacific 太平洋的一个偏僻海岛

removable
/rɪˈmu:vəbl ||; rɪˈmuvəbḷ/adj (usually before a noun 通常用于名词前) that can be taken off or out of sth 可移掉的；能取出的 [SYN] detachable 同义词为detachable

*remove
/rɪˈmu:v ||; rɪˈmuv/verb [T] (formal 正式)
1 remove sb/sth (from sth) to take sb/sth off or away 移开；拿走；除去；消除: Remove the saucepan from the heat. 把平底锅从火上拿下来。 This washing powder will remove most stains. 这种洗衣粉可除去大部份污渍。 to remove doubts/fears/problems 消除疑虑╱恐惧╱问题 I would like you to remove my name from your mailing list. 请把我的名字从你们的邮寄名单中删除。 He had an operation to remove the tumour. 他动了一次手术，切除肿瘤。 ☞ Take off, out, etc is less formal. take off／out等多用于非正式场合。
2 remove sb (from sth) to make sb leave his/her job or position 开除；解雇；免去某人的职务

removed
/rɪˈmu:vd ||; rɪˈmuvd/adj (not before a noun 不用于名词前) far or different from sth 远离；不相同: Hospitals today are far removed from what they were fifty years ago. 今天的医院与五十年前的已大不相同了。

renew
/rɪˈnju:; US -ˈnu: ||; rɪˈnu/verb[T]
1 to start sth again 重新开始: renewed outbreaks of violence 暴力事件的再度爆发 to renew a friendship 重修旧好
2 to give sb new strength or energy 使重新充满力量: After a break he set to work with renewed enthusiasm. 休息了一会儿后，他又干劲十足地继续工作。
3 to make sth valid for a further period of time 使有效期延长: to renew a contract/passport/library book 续约；使护照展期；续借图书馆的书 ➔renewal /-ˈnju:əl; US -ˈnu:əl ||; -ˈnuəl/ noun [C,U] When is your passport due for renewal? 你的护照什么时候应当展期？

renewable
/rɪˈnju:əbl ||; rɪˈnuəbḷ/adj
1 (used about sources of energy) that will always exist （指能源）可再生的: renewable resources such as wind and solar power 风力和太阳能等再生能源 [OPP] non-renewable 反义词为non-renewable
2 that can be continued or replaced with a new one for another period of time 可继续一段时期的；可更换的

renounce
/rɪˈnaʊns ||; rɪˈnaυns/verb [T] (formal 正式) to say formally that you no longer want to have sth or to be connected with sth 正式声明放弃某物；正式声明与…断绝关系 ☞noun renunciation 名词为renunciation

renovate
/ˈrenəveɪt ||; ˈrɛnəˌvet/verb [T] to repair an old building and put it back into good condition 修复，修葺，翻新（旧建筑物） ➔renovation /ˌrenəˈveɪʃn ||; ˌrɛnəˈveʃən/ noun [C,U] The house is in need of complete renovation. 这房子需要全面修葺。

renown
/rɪˈnaʊn ||; rɪˈnaυn/noun [U] (formal 正式) fame and respect that you get for doing sth especially well 名望；声誉 ➔renowned adj renowned (for/as sth) The region is renowned for its food. 该地区以美食见称。

*rent¹
/rent ||; rɛnt/noun [U] [C] money that you pay regularly for the use of land, a house or a building 租金；房租: a high/low rent 昂贵的／便宜的租金 She was allowed to live there rent-free until she found a job. 她被准许免交房租住在那里，直到她找到工作。 Is this house for rent (= available to rent)? 这房子出租吗？
*rent²
/rent ||; rɛnt/verb[T]
1 rent sth (from sb) to pay money for the use of land, a building, a machine, etc 租用；租借: Do you own or rent your television? 你的电视机是自己的还是租的？ to rent a flat 租一套公寓 ☞ Look at the note at hire ¹(1). 参看hire^1(1)的注释。
2 rent sth (out) (to sb) to allow sb to use land, a building, a machine, etc for money （向某人）出租（土地、建筑物、机器等）: We could rent out the small bedroom to a student. 我们可以把那间小卧室租给一个学生。 ☞Look at hire ¹(3). 参看hire^1(3)。
3 (US 美) =HIRE¹(1)
4 (US 美) =HIRE¹(3)

reopen
/ˌri:ˈəʊpən ||; riˈopən/verb[T]
1 to open a shop/store, theatre, etc again, or to be opened again, after being closed for a period of time 重新开业；重新开放: The school was reopened just two weeks after the fire. 火灾之后仅两个星期，这所学校就重新开学了。 The store will reopen at 9 a.m. on January 2. 商店将于元月 2 号上午 9 点重新开业。
2 to deal with or begin sth again after a period of time; to start again after a period of time 重新处理；再次开始；恢复: to reopen an argument/a discussion/a debate 重新开始争论/讨论/辩论 The police have decided to reopen the case. 警方已经决定重新审理这个案子了。
reopen old wounds to remind sb of sth unpleasant that happened or existed in the past 揭旧伤疤 ➔reopening noun [U,sing]

*repair¹
/rɪˈpeə(r) ||; rɪˈpɛr/verb [T] to put sth old or damaged back into good condition 修理；修补: These cars can be expensive to repair. 这些汽车修理起来费用可能很贵。 How much will it cost to have the TV repaired? 修理这台电视机要多少钱？ [SYN] fix or mend 同义词为fix或mend ☞ Look at irreparable. 参看irreparable。
